### 1. 火车广告风格的书籍广告图片

**作者**: [KAWAI](https://x.com/kawai_design/status/1992142466255114727)  **日期**: 2025-11-22  **语言**: ja

> 一个详细的日文提示，用于生成一个 16:9 的商业书籍风格广告，其中包含特定书籍图片和日文文案要点。

![火车广告风格的书籍广告图片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763885539326_yao7in_G6WBYReawAAcp2x.jpg)

```
広告画像を生成してください

==== 広告の仕様 ===
- アスペクト比: 16:9（横長）
- 広告したい商品: 添付画像1枚目の本
- アイキャッチ: 添付画像1枚目の本を立体的に配置
- 使用言語: 日本語
- テイスト: ビジネス書の広告

# 掲載文字:
- プリデッドコピー: | 【 発売1週間ほどで重版決定 】

書籍「{argument name="書籍名" default="AIでゼロからデザイン"}」好評発売中

Amazon 売れ筋ランキング
商業デザイン売上 1位 を記録（10/15 調べ）
https://t.co/QxbYpfFVj6
```

**Related**: [[综合3D]]

### 2. Ghormeh Sabzi 的中世纪祭坛画展示

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2038647691358478407)  **日期**: 2026-03-30  **语言**: en

> 这是一个复杂的多面板提示词，旨在将国际美食（Ghormeh Sabzi）呈现为中世纪祭坛画。它详细说明了三个面板的结构，要求包含食材标本、3D 立体透视模型以及以 3D 设计师玩具风格呈现的烹饪步骤，所有内容均置于博物馆展览场景中。

![Ghormeh Sabzi 的中世纪祭坛画展示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774939639285_clddgz_HEd1ZZRaAAAnsZB.jpg)

```
<instruction> Input A is a famous dish (photo or dish name). Analyze the dish's ingredient taxonomy, preparation methodology, cultural preparation setting, and historical documentation style.
Optional Input B is a style reference (3d mod designer toy luxury product packaging).  
Goal: Three-panel folding display (12" tall, 36" wide when open) structured like a medieval altarpiece, with each panel revealing different aspects of the dish's story through museum-quality presentation.
Rules:
Left panel: 15-20 ingredients mounted as specimens in tiny bottles with handwritten Latin/scientific labels
Center panel: 3D pop-up kitchen diorama with cultural figure preparing dish, architectural elements from origin region
Right panel: 6-8 precise preparation steps as 3D mod designer toy style
Closes into protective case with magnetic closure and embossed exterior
Exterior: ornate typography with dish name in gold foil
Small drawer at base containing actual spice sample or "secret ingredient"
Color palette drawn from traditional pottery/textiles of origin culture
Include tiny rolled "scroll" with full recipe in calligraphy
Output: ONE image, 16:9 showing triptych fully opened, shot straight-on, museum exhibition lighting </instruction>
```

**Related**: [[像素艺术]]、[[微缩模型与立体模型]]、[[综合3D]]

### 3. 带有建筑工人的茶杯微距产品照

**作者**: [Shah](https://x.com/ai_with_shah/status/2036476531048907066)  **日期**: 2026-03-24  **语言**: en

> 生成一张超逼真的 8K 微距产品照片的提示词：画面主体是一个巨大的透明玻璃茶杯，伴随着戏剧性的凝固热茶飞溅。场景中，迷你建筑工人正在杯沿上爬梯子，并在茶碟上清扫。画面强调蒸汽颗粒、琥珀色液体质感和高对比度的摄影棚灯光。

![带有建筑工人的茶杯微距产品照](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421478553_9n3wi0_HEMEE4fWYAAwWG6.jpg)

![带有建筑工人的茶杯微距产品照](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421478606_4o9hyy_HEMEE4pXQAAkqjc.jpg)
![带有建筑工人的茶杯微距产品照](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421479387_b7j0lb_HEMEE4eXQAAb5pu.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": "Ultra-realistic 8K macro product shot, pure white background. Giant transparent glass teacup with dramatic hot tea splash frozen mid-air. Tiny construction workers in yellow helmets climbing ladders on the rim, sweeping the saucer. Steam particles rising, rich amber liquid texture, dramatic studio lighting with high-contrast shadows and reflections",
  "negative_prompt": "blurry, people faces, text"
}
```

### 4. Nano Banana Pro 的 Noir Techcore 产品摄影提示词

**作者**: [Lloyd Creates](https://x.com/lloydcreates/status/2035740443007209485)  **日期**: 2026-03-22  **语言**: en

> 这是一条为 Nano Banana Pro 精心设计的结构化、高细节提示词，旨在生成超写实的黑色科技风（Noir Techcore）产品摄影图。它规定了严格的构图规则、带有橙色和琥珀色光泽的戏剧性轮廓光，以及一系列详尽的负面约束条件，以确保画面呈现出纯净、专业的真空氛围感。

![Nano Banana Pro 的 Noir Techcore 产品摄影提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334476798_722pxn_HEBnGyZXEAIIs5x.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_request": {
    "subject_configuration": {
      "placeholder": "{argument name=\"product name\" default=\"[INSERT_PRODUCT_HERE]\"}",
      "positioning": "strictly_centered",
      "presentation": "levitating_in_void",
      "composition_rules": [
        "entire_product_visible",
        "no_cropping",
        "zero_edge_clipping",
        "subject_must_be_contained_within_frame_safety_margins"
      ]
    },
    "environment_and_lighting": {
      "background_color": "#000000",
      "lighting_style": "dramatic_rim_lighting",
      "primary_glow_color": "{argument name=\"primary glow color\" default=\"#FF4500\"}",
      "accent_lighting": "mechanical_internal_luminescence",
      "surface_textures": [
        "anodized_black_metal",
        "iridescent_glass_reflections",
        "crystalline_transparency",
        "carbon_fiber_matte"
      ]
    },
    "visual_effects": {
      "style_blend": "Hyper-realistic_Industrial_Design",
      "mechanical_detail": "macro_lens_precision",
      "atmosphere": "clean_vacuum_void"
    },
    "negative_constraints": {
      "prohibited_elements": [
        "text",
        "typography",
        "logos",
        "watermarks",
        "pedestals",
        "stands",
        "mounting_brackets",
        "visible_light_boxes",
        "softbox_reflections",
        "studio_props",
        "background_gradients",
        "floor_planes",
        "shadow_casting_on_surfaces"
      ],
      "framing_errors": [
        "cut_off_edges",
        "zoomed_in",
        "partial_view",
        "off-center"
      ]
    },
    "color_palette_specification": {
      "base": "#000000",
      "highlight_orange": "#FF5E00",
      "amber_glow": "#CC4400",
      "steel_accent": "#A8A8A8"
    }
  }
}
```

### 5. Enka CD 封面设计与 Nano Banana 2

**作者**: [なお](https://x.com/Naonekozamurai/status/2033660646731247730)  **日期**: 2026-03-16  **语言**: ja

> 为 Nano Banana 2 提供一个详细的提示，用于创建一张演歌（日本传统民谣）风格的 CD 封面，并使用一张人物参考图片。该提示详细说明了设计元素、戏剧性氛围、标题要求（演歌风格、毛笔字体）以及要排除的元素（条形码、徽标等）。

![Enka CD 封面设计与 Nano Banana 2](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773729536008_9dpnzm_HDkB0VvbEAALDpd.jpg)
![Enka CD 封面设计与 Nano Banana 2](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773729536000_7f776h_HDkBxkUaoAASriN.jpg)
![Enka CD 封面设计与 Nano Banana 2](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773729536040_i80rig_HDkBzDqbgAAXacn.jpg)
![Enka CD 封面设计与 Nano Banana 2](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773729536860_2js86a_HDkB10QaoAA8G_D.jpg)

```
リファレンス画像に写っている人物を同一人物として使用し、その人物がリリースした「演歌のCDジャケット」をデザインしてください。

重要:
・人物の顔や特徴はリファレンス画像から忠実に再現する
・元画像の構図、カメラアングル、ポーズ、背景には縛られない
・新しくCDジャケット用に構図を大胆に再構成する
・実在する演歌CDジャケットのような完成度の高いデザインにする

デザイン要素:
・演歌らしいドラマチックで情緒的な雰囲気
・昭和～現代演歌のCDジャケットのようなデザイン
・人物は中央または印象的な配置
・強い感情表現（哀愁、決意、切なさなど）
・背景は自由に変更してよい。演歌の世界観を表現する情緒的でドラマチックな背景にすること。

タイトル:
・リファレンス画像の人物の雰囲気やキャラクターから推測して
「それらしい演歌のタイトル」を新しく作る
・タイトルは大きくジャケットに表示する
・演歌風の日本語タイトル
・筆文字風フォント

追加要素:
・本物のCDジャケットのようなレイアウト
・高品質、印刷用レベルのクオリティ

スタイル:
日本の演歌CDジャケット
ドラマチックなライティング
映画ポスターのような構図
高解像度
プロのグラフィックデザイン

以下の要素は一切表示しない：
・バーコード
・価格表示
・JANコード
・レコード会社ロゴ
・CDレーベルロゴ
・コピーライト表記
・発売日
・型番
・商品番号
・キャンペーンシール
・ステッカー
・宣伝バッジ
・帯（オビ）
・販売用ラベル
・ストリーミングサービスのロゴ
・Spotify / Apple Music などのアイコン
・QRコード

文字情報は「演歌タイトル」と「歌手名」のみ表示すること。「サブタイトル」は表示してもよい。
それ以外の文字・記号・数字は一切表示しない。
商業CDパッケージに見られる販売情報はすべて禁止。
```

**Related**: [[电影海报]]、[[贴纸]]、[[综合设计]]

### 6. 产品组装顺序时间表

**作者**: [Alexandra Aisling](https://x.com/AllaAisling/status/2033218108433809587)  **日期**: 2026-03-15  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂的多阶段提示，专为 Nano Banana 2（在 Adobe Firefly 中使用）设计，用于生成一个 5 格水平时间轴，展示产品组装顺序，重点是戏剧性照明、技术精确性和一致的摄像机角度。

![产品组装顺序时间表](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773643976636_wiorx9_HDdwJpKXoAAU_He.jpg)
![产品组装顺序时间表](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773643976742_02299d_HDdv2qpWcAAjiia.jpg)
![产品组装顺序时间表](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773643976909_okb2bb_HDdwtrdWsAEaWaC.jpg)
![产品组装顺序时间表](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773643977504_81eh7o_HDdxC-xXUAA1QLl.jpg)

```
5-stage horizontal manufacturing timeline, frozen mid-assembly. deep matte black background. dramatic industrial spotlights, deep shadow falloff.  
S1: Components scattered, floating, zero assembly. 
S2: Converging with speed lines, skeleton emerging. 
S3: Half-built, peak tension, fasteners mid-tighten. 
S4: Chassis open, full internals exposed. 
S5: Finished product + ghost wireframe overlay.  
Same 3/4 camera angle across all stages. Dotted trajectory arcs connect each component across stages. Each component color-coded consistently.  Title: "PRODUCT NAME - ASSEMBLY SEQUENCE" Footer: "N parts parts · X hrs · KEY SPEC"  Helvetica Neue Light labels. 4K, tack sharp. Dieter Rams precision.
```

### 7. 高对比度跪姿再现提示

**作者**: [Jessia](https://x.com/itsjessiababy/status/2032416402150232394)  **日期**: 2026-03-13  **语言**: en

> 这是一个极其详细、结构化的 JSON 提示，专为 Nano Banana Pro 设计，侧重于图像再现和精确的姿态几何。它描述了一位年轻女子跪在柏油路上，穿着特定的服装，化着浓妆，头部被一只外来的手向后拉。该提示指定了高角度、倾斜的构图，以及与夜间停车场环境相符的刺眼、高对比度的人造照明。

![高对比度跪姿再现提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773469806067_za5jbz_HDSX6l-XQAA-__M.jpg)

{
  "image_reproduction_prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Young woman with long, straight dark brown hair, olive skin tone, and heavy makeup featuring prominent pink circular blush on the cheeks, glossy pink lips, and long dark eyelashes.       "spine_and_pelvis": "Deep lumbar arch with the upper torso leaning back; the spine forms a diagonal C-curve from the pelvis to the neck. Pelvis is tilted forward and shifted slightly to the subject's left.",
      "head_and_neck": "Head is tilted sharply back and rotated toward the left shoulder; neck is elongated and strained. An external male hand is visible in the upper right frame, gripping a thick clump of the subject's hair near the crown and pulling it upward and toward the right.",
      "shoulders": "Asymmetrical height; the right shoulder is raised and pulled back by the tension on the hair, while the left shoulder is dropped lower and pushed forward.",
      "arms": "Right arm is angled down and slightly away from the body; left arm is positioned straight down toward the ground, though the hands are cut off by the bottom frame.",
      "legs_and_weight": "Kneeling position with knees spread wide; weight is distributed heavily onto the knees and shins. The lower body is angled toward the bottom left of the frame.",
      "contact_points": "Knees and shins in firm contact with the asphalt; external hand in tight contact with the hair at the scalp."
    },
    "camera_configuration": {
      "angle": "High-angle shot looking down at the subject.",
      "tilt": "Slightly canted/Dutch angle, tilted toward the left.",
      "distance": "Medium-close-up, focusing on the upper body and head.",
      "perspective": "Incidental, amateur-style framing with the external arm entering from the top right edge."
    },
    "lighting_and_physics": {
      "type": "Harsh, direct artificial lighting consistent with outdoor parking lot floodlights at night.",

      "shadows": "Hard-edged shadow cast onto the asphalt directly behind and to the left of the subject."
    },
    "environment_and_color": {
      "background": "An
```

### 8. Nano Banana 2 的 3D 径向爆炸产品可视化提示

**作者**: [Alexandra Aisling](https://x.com/AllaAisling/status/2032126653309030481)  **日期**: 2026-03-12  **语言**: en

> 为 Nano Banana 2 设计的高度结构化提示，旨在创建产品超逼真的 3D 径向爆炸图，详细说明组件层、材料、照明和特定标签要求，风格介于 iFixit 拆解和 NASA 手册之间。

![Nano Banana 2 的 3D 径向爆炸产品可视化提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773383490311_9hkect_HDOPlsPX0AAdu1e.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 的 3D 径向爆炸产品可视化提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773383490317_q8mnfv_HDOQI1QagAAyGdc.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 的 3D 径向爆炸产品可视化提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773383490311_z2btkz_HDOPxHCWQAI7drR.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 的 3D 径向爆炸产品可视化提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773383491016_39n75z_HDOQS2xWcAA8dbq.jpg)

```
Hyperrealistic 3D radial exploded view of {argument name="product" default="PRODUCT"}  {argument name="number of components" default="NUMBER"} components  bursting outward from a central axis in every direction, frozen in mid-air.  True spatial explosion, not a vertical stack, depth and parallax visible.  COMPONENTS (core outward): {argument name="shell material" default="SHELL"} → DISPLAY → FRAME → MAINBOARD →  BATTERY → MICRO PARTS shown in 3x floating callout circles  MATERIALS: glass refracts and catches specular highlights, aluminium shows  brushed grain and machined edges, PCB traces glow faintly amber,   rubber gaskets matte with micro-texture, cables with soft bend physics.  LABELS: hairline leader to floating box. "[COMPONENT]" uppercase /  "[FUNCTION]" italic / "[KEY SPEC]" monospace. Radiate outward, no overlaps.  LIGHTING: cool diffused overhead + warm amber underlighting on internals +  thin blue rim on outer shell. Displays emit soft UI glow. Circuits self-illuminate.  BACKGROUND: {argument name="background color" default="COLOR"}, deep, non-reflective. Midnight black recommended. TITLE: "[PRODUCT NAME]" top right. SUBTITLE: "[TAGLINE]".  SPEC BLOCK: "[SPEC 1] / [SPEC 2] / [SPEC 3]" bottom left in monospace.  Mood: iFixit teardown meets NASA manual meets WIRED cover. 4K, tack sharp, extraordinary material fidelity.
```

### 9. 高转化率广告图片的通用提示词

**作者**: [みゆ【重要AIニュースを毎日配信⚡】](https://x.com/miyu_AI_usa/status/2031516902145798616)  **日期**: 2026-03-10  **语言**: ja

> 一个专为 Nano Banana (Pro) 设计的通用提示，它能帮助销售专业人士通过首先研究日本市场中成功的广告设计，然后将这些成功的模式应用于生成过程，从而创建高转化率的广告图片。

```
日本市場の同ジャンルで伸びている広告デザインをリサーチし、勝ちパターンを抽出して、【{argument name="媒体" default="ココに媒体を書く"}】広告を作って。商品のCV最大化を狙う広告画像を生成して。【{argument name="サイズ指定" default="サイズ指定"}】で作って。
```

### 10. Y2K Chrome 毛绒产品渲染图

**作者**: [Lloyd Creates](https://x.com/lloydcreates/status/2030385497260831000)  **日期**: 2026-03-07  **语言**: en

> 一个高度技术化的 JSON 提示词，用于生成一个 8k Octane 渲染的产品（占位符），其风格融合了超逼真的毛绒人造毛皮和熔融的虹彩液态铬，并带有参数化 3D 切片几何。它指定了一个严格居中、悬浮的主体，置于纯黑背景之上，使用影棚级轮廓光和充满活力的 Y2K 强调色。

![Y2K Chrome 毛绒产品渲染图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772951297992_4rirtd_HC1gnodWAAAzbti.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_request": {
    "subject": {
      "placeholder": "{argument name="product name" default="[INSERT_PRODUCT_NAME_HERE]"}",
      "positioning": "strictly centered, floating, levitating, full view, no cropping, entire object visible within frame",
      "scale": "0.8x of frame height to ensure no edge-cut"
    },
    "stylization_blend": {
      "geometry": "parametric 3D sliced layers, vertical rhythmic ribs, undulating waveform distortions across the surface",
      "textures": [
        "hyper-realistic plush faux fur with soft tactile fibers",
        "molten iridescent liquid chrome with high-viscosity surface tension",
        "holographic dispersion and spectral color shifts on metallic edges"
      ],
      "material_properties": "fusion of soft-touch textile and hard-surface refractive glass-metal"
    },
    "environment": {
      "background": "absolute solid pitch black, hex code #000000, void",
      "lighting": "studio-quality rim lighting, internal glow, prismatic refraction, no visible light sources",
      "platforms": "none, no stands, no pedestals, no floor, no shadows on ground"
    },
    "color_palette": {
      "primary_background": "#000000",
      "accent_colors": [
        "#0000FF (Electric Blue)",
        "#FFD700 (Gold)",
        "#00FFC8 (Hyper-Cyan)",
        "#FF00FF (Vivid Magenta)"
      ],
      "shading": "high contrast, deep shadows, vibrant saturated highlights"
    },
    "negative_constraints": {
      "elements_to_exclude": [
        "text", "labels", "watermarks", "logos", "lighting boxes", "softboxes", "tripods", "camera gear", 
        "platforms", "tables", "pedestals", "mannequin limbs", "props", "dust", "scratches", 
        "out of frame", "cropped edges", "depth of field blur on product", "room background", "walls"
      ],
      "visual_errors": "cut off parts, clipping, extra appendages, distorted geometry beyond intended artistic ripple"
    },
    "technical_specs": {
      "rendering_style": "8k octane render, unreal engine 5.4, ray-traced reflections, photorealistic, clean minimalist aesthetic",
      "aspect_ratio": "1:1"
    }
  }
}
```

### 11. 奢华产品营销活动网格

**作者**: [Ashley 🆇](https://x.com/Ashlley_grace_/status/2029881440712978701)  **日期**: 2026-03-06  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的结构化 JSON 提示，旨在为奢华产品广告系列生成 3x3 的图像网格。它指定了九种不同的拍摄类型（例如，主打静物、微距纹理、超现实融合），同时保持产品一致性、简洁背景和柔和的影棚照明。

![奢华产品营销活动网格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772864631064_6iorvf_HCuWZ2uaYAEwJPc.jpg)

{
  "prompt": {
    "layout": {
      "type": "grid",
      "rows": 3,
      "columns": 3,
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5"
    },
    "style": "luxury campaign",
    "product": {
      "placement": "centered",
      "consistency": "same product across all 9 shots"
    },
    "shots": [
      {
        "position": 1,
        "type": "hero still life"
      },
      {
        "position": 2,
        "type": "macro texture"
      },
      {
        "position": 3,
        "type": "liquid or particles"
      },
      {
        "position": 4,
        "type": "minimal sculptural"
      },
      {
        "position": 5,
        "type": "floating"
      },
      {
        "position": 6,
        "type": "tactile close-up"
      },
      {
        "position": 7,
        "type": "color-driven"
      },
      {
        "position": 8,
        "type": "abstract ingredient"
      },
      {
        "position": 9,
        "type": "surreal fusion"
      }
    ],

      "no_distortion": true,
      "no_label_changes": true,

**作者**: [LexiPrompt](https://x.com/Artist04048661/status/2029294271879168502)  **日期**: 2026-03-04  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超逼真的年轻女性图像，该女性酷似 Sabrina Carpenter，身穿比基尼和珠宝，坐在一个质朴的水果摊位旁，手持一片西瓜，强调直射阳光和高对比度阴影。

      "style": "Bohemian Summer / Coastal Chic."
    },

        "Layered gold necklaces with various eclectic charms and pendants",

        "A chunky translucent pink ring",

    },

Top-down camera angle (exactly as in the image).

### 17. 超逼真产品渲染，搭配 Holochrome 渐变

**作者**: [Lloyd Creates](https://x.com/lloydcreates/status/2028852538443743580)  **日期**: 2026-03-03  **语言**: en

> 一个用于生成超逼真 8K 产品渲染图的高度技术性提示。它在灯光（硬边缘光、轮廓光、明暗对比）、材质（拉丝铝、镜面镀铬）和构图（居中、悬浮在纯黑虚空中）方面指定了极致的细节，同时严格禁止常见的摄影元素。

![超逼真产品渲染，搭配 Holochrome 渐变](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772605586143_0xb7bg_HCfukwtWsAAqFSp.jpg)

```
Create a hyper-realistic 8K product render of {argument name="product name" default="[INSERT YOUR PRODUCT HERE]"}

The subject should be perfectly centered and levitating in mid-air, floating in a void with no surface, platform, stand, or floor. Show the full product with zero cropping and visible margins on all sides. 
Use a dynamic macro 45-degree hero angle.

The background must be solid pure black (#000000).

Lighting should feature hard edge lighting with strong rim light highlights. Use a high-contrast chiaroscuro look with thin chromatic aberration along metallic edges. Include reflective caustic light hits and an oily iridescent sheen on polished surfaces.

Color palette:

Background: #000000
Metal highlights: #E0E0E0
Iridescent accents: #4169E1, #FFD700, #FF4500

Materials and textures should combine micro-brushed sandblasted aluminum with mirror-finish chrome. Add subtle prismatic dispersion and thin-film interference along metal curves. Include fine film grain for tactile realism.

Do not include any props or additional objects. 
No light boxes, umbrellas, softboxes, pedestals, cables, tripods, or hands. 
No cropped edges or cut-off parts. 
No text, logos, watermarks, blur, bokeh background, dust, or scratches.

Style reference: Industrial Design meets luxury hardware photography.
```

### 24. 技术信息图解剖面图提示

**作者**: [Weinberg](https://x.com/weiinberg/status/2027986208408977548)  **日期**: 2026-03-01  **语言**: en

> 一个用于生成物体高分辨率、专业技术信息图的提示模板。它需要一个清晰、半写实的剖面图，展示内部组件，并自动标注技术术语，以及一个适合工程手册的平衡布局。

![技术信息图解剖面图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433492844_q6zr64_HCTasgQaYAADK5w.jpg)
![技术信息图解剖面图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433492828_rtz9na_HCTasgVacAEMa7s.jpg)
![技术信息图解剖面图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433493530_9ulyhy_HCTasgRa4AAh2YG.jpg)
![技术信息图解剖面图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433493769_1405cw_HCTasgQbEAEuwwx.jpg)

```
Create a high-resolution professional infographic of [{argument name="object name" default="OBJECT NAME"}].
Display the object in a clean, semi-realistic technical illustration style. Include both external structure and internal components using a cutaway view, cross-section, or exploded layout where appropriate.
Automatically detect and label all major structural, mechanical, electronic, or functional components using accurate technical terminology.
Use thin leader lines connecting each label precisely to the correct part. Ensure labels are clear, readable, and professionally formatted.
Add a bold headline at the top:
“OBJECT NAME – Complete Structural Breakdown”
Layout should be balanced and organized like a modern engineering manual or product teardown poster.
Background: clean white or light neutral tone.
Lighting: neutral studio lighting with soft shadows for depth.
Materials and textures must look realistic and detailed.
Use modern sans-serif typography with clear hierarchy (bold headings, smaller technical labels).
Ultra-detailed, sharp focus, 4K resolution, professional educational infographic style.
No artistic distortion, no clutter, no decorative elements unrelated to structure.
```

### 32. 面向对象的科技信息图表模板

**作者**: [Edraak Tech | إدراك تِك](https://x.com/EdraakTechAi/status/2026095651256181079)  **日期**: 2026-02-24  **语言**: en

> 一个模板提示，用于创建任何对象的科技信息图，采用 45 度等距 3D 透视，结合照片级真实感、黑色墨水注释以及用于功能/流程的颜色编码箭头。

![面向对象的科技信息图表模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772001512625_1omobh_HB4jNMqXQAAQHJE.jpg)
![面向对象的科技信息图表模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772001512780_i7a0s3_HB4jNLvWgAALsmW.jpg)
![面向对象的科技信息图表模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772001512653_wu5r6i_HB4jNL1XkAAa_CV.jpg)
![面向对象的科技信息图表模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772001514012_n92c2t_HB4jNMYWMAEDohe.jpg)

```
Create a technical infographic of {argument name="object name" default="[OBJECT NAME]"} with a 45-degree isometric 3D perspective showing the device slightly tilted to reveal depth and dimension.
Combine a realistic photoreal render with black ink technical annotations on pure white background. Include:
Key component labels with color-coded callout boxes Internal component visibility through transparent/cutaway sections
Measurements, dimensions, and precise scale markers Material callouts and quantities 
Color-coded arrows for function/flow: RED (power/battery), BLUE (data/connectivity), ORANGE (thermal/processor), GREEN (sensors/haptics)
Simple schematics or cross-sectional diagrams where relevant 
Place “OBJECT NAME” title in a hand-drawn technical box (top-left corner).
Style: Black linework (technical pen/architectural), sketched but precise. Object remains clearly visible. Educational museum-exhibit vibe. Clean composition, balanced negative space.
Perspective: Isometric 3D angle—tilted to show depth, dimension, and internal architecture dramatically. Like a professional product teardown or engineering manual.
Colors: ~10–15% accent density. Black dominant. White background.
Output: 1080×1080, ultra-crisp, social-feed optimized.
```

### 38. 废弃古老丛林城市的电影概念艺术

**作者**: [Artingent](https://x.com/artingent/status/2023834163066138892)  **日期**: 2026-02-17  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的主提示，旨在生成古老、废弃的丛林城市广场的高端电影风格写实概念艺术，重点是深层环境分层、清晨光线透过树冠的过滤，以及一种古老发现的感觉。

![废弃古老丛林城市的电影概念艺术](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771396579008_cv0xlk_HBYabuFbcAc6Oag.jpg)

```
ONE-CLICK GENERIC MASTER PROMPT — ANCIENT JUNGLE MORNING
STYLE
High-end cinematic stylized-realism digital concept art, AAA environment
keyframe illustration, film matte-painting depth construction, professional
game environment rendering, minimal line art, value-driven form separation,
painted edges, controlled edge hierarchy, large-to-small mass construction,
clean gradient digital color blending, hybrid hand-painted procedural texture,
macro readability prioritized with selective micro-detail in focal structures,
studio-quality composition, polished senior-level production finish.
SUBJECT / SCENE
In an Ancient Jungle Morning Setting, a long-abandoned jungle city plaza with cracked statues and vine-covered arches.
ENVIRONMENT
Primeval overgrown jungle landscape with monumental ancient natural formations,
dense layered vegetation, colossal trees, tangled roots, mist-filled clearings,
hidden stone remnants or forgotten pathways partially reclaimed by nature.
Large readable terrain masses first, with deep environmental layering and
strong spatial separation between foreground foliage, mid jungle structures,
and distant canopy silhouettes.
LIGHTING
Fresh early-morning jungle illumination with low-angle sunlight filtering
through dense canopy gaps in structured directional shafts. Light should
clearly define major structural planes while allowing gentle atmospheric mist
to separate depth layers and enhance spatial readability without obscuring
primary forms.
CAMERA
Cinematic exploration-style wide establishing shot positioned slightly above
ground level as if the viewer has just discovered the scene. Use natural
foreground framing through vegetation or terrain forms, clear midground focal
anchor, and deep layered jungle distance to reinforce cinematic matte-painting
depth construction.
MOOD
Sense of ancient discovery, untouched history, and quiet natural majesty.
The scene should feel like the first reveal of a lost jungle location in a
high-budget adventure film or AAA exploration game.
DETAIL CONTROL
Maintain professional focal-detail hierarchy. Preserve large readable jungle
masses first, secondary structural forms next, and apply fine detail only in
primary focal regions. Avoid uniform high-frequency foliage noise or excessive
micro-detail in distant canopy layers.
QUALITY TARGET
Ultra-clean studio-grade cinematic jungle environment illustration, portfolio-
level concept art readability, strong depth hierarchy, and polished production-
ready rendering quality.
```

**Related**: [[手绘素描]]、[[综合艺术]]、[[圣诞节]]

```
SHORT STRUCTURED PROMPT — CINEMATIC OBSERVATORY TEST
STYLE
High-end cinematic stylized-realism digital concept art, AAA environment
keyframe illustration, film matte-painting depth construction, professional
game environment rendering, minimal line art, value-driven form separation,
painted edges, controlled edge hierarchy, large-to-small mass construction,
clean gradient digital color blending, hybrid hand-painted procedural texture,

studio-quality composition, polished senior-level production finish.

circular astronomical device embedded in the rock wall.

Vast mountainous frontier with deep forest valleys, winding river systems,

Early morning directional sunlight defining major planes clearly, gentle

secondary structures next, fine detail only in anchor regions, avoid uniform

### 40. 技术信息图表提示模板

**作者**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X/status/2023610125249044854)  **日期**: 2026-02-17  **语言**: en

> 一个可复用的提示模板，用于生成对象的工程技术信息图，特点是 45 度等距 3D 视角、黑色墨迹注释、剖面图、尺寸标注以及用于功能/流程的颜色编码箭头，风格类似于工程手册。

![技术信息图表提示模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771396580715_rvug9m_HBVOp5kboAAI6xv.jpg)
![技术信息图表提示模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771396580708_7butuk_HBVOp5sbcAUM-Kh.jpg)

```
Create a technical infographic of {argument name="object" default="OBJECT"} with a 45-degree isometric 3D perspective showing the device slightly tilted to reveal depth and dimension.
Combine a realistic photoreal render with black ink technical annotations on pure white background. Include:
Key component labels with color-coded callout boxes
Internal component visibility through transparent/cutaway sections
Measurements, dimensions, and precise scale markers
Material callouts and quantities
Color-coded arrows for function/flow: RED (power/battery), BLUE (data/connectivity), ORANGE (thermal/processor), GREEN (sensors/haptics)
Simple schematics or cross-sectional diagrams where relevant

Place “OBJECT” title in a hand-drawn technical box (top-left corner).
Style: Black linework (technical pen/architectural), sketched but precise. Object remains clearly visible. Educational museum-exhibit vibe. Clean composition, balanced negative space.
Perspective: Isometric 3D angle—tilted to show depth, dimension, and internal architecture dramatically. Like a professional product teardown or engineering manual.
Colors: ~10-15% accent density. Black dominant. White background.
Output: 1080×1080, ultra-crisp, social-feed optimized.
```

**Related**: [[手绘素描]]、[[3D渲染]]、[[综合3D]]

### 43. 照片转画布艺术品提示

**作者**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1/status/2022439710011072990)  **日期**: 2026-02-13  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂、结构化的 JSON 提示词，旨在将上传的夫妻照片转换为仅有方形画布的油画艺术作品，采用丙烯插画风格，具有可见的画布纹理、简洁的线条以及浪漫、温暖的色调。

![照片转画布艺术品提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771050434823_xykpmh_HBEmMEhakAA06JK.jpg)
![照片转画布艺术品提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771050434949_mxe46z_HBEmMEdakAA2dto.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "task_type": "photo_to_square_canvas_artwork_only",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.1_DIRECT_CANVAS_ART_ONLY"
    },
    "input": {
      "mode": "image_to_image",
      "reference_image_usage": "very_high",
      "preserve_identity": true,
      "preserve_facial_features": true,
      "notes": "Transform the uploaded couple photo into a square canvas painting artwork only. No product setup. The final image should be just the painted canvas design itself, centered and clean. Keep the couple recognizable but simplified into a warm hand-drawn illustration style."
    },
    "output": {
      "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
      "resolution": "ultra_high",
      "num_images": 2,
      "sharpness": "high",
      "grain": "subtle_canvas_texture"
    },
    "canvas_art_style": {
      "art_medium": "acrylic illustration on canvas",
      "texture": "visible canvas fabric weave",
      "linework": "clean ink outline",
      "coloring": "soft painted fills with gentle shading",
      "finish": "real hand-painted canvas look"
    },
    "canvas_design": {
      "background_color": "muted lavender or soft pastel tone",
      "pattern": "small scattered white or light heart doodles",
      "couple_pose": "romantic close seated embrace similar to uploaded photo",
      "edge_detail": "subtle white outline around couple illustration"
    },
    "subject_rules": {
      "identity": "match the uploaded couple’s facial structure and hair",
      "expressions": "warm affectionate smiles with soft blush",
      "hands": "correct anatomy, natural interaction",
      "wardrobe_translation": "simplified illustrated version of original outfits"
    },
    "composition": {
      "centered": true,
      "clean_background": true,
      "no_external_objects": true
    },
    "negative_prompt": [
      "product photography",
      "easel",
      "wood slice",
      "candle",
      "room background",
      "3d render",
      "anime style",
      "watercolor wash",
      "text",
      "logo",
      "watermark",
      "extra fingers",
      "deformed hands",
      "blurry"
    ],
    "quality_rules": {
      "must": [
        "only the square canvas artwork visible",
        "canvas texture clearly visible",
        "couple recognizable",
        "clean illustration lines",
        "romantic warm tone",
        "no extra objects around"
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

### 44. Chrome Ripple Flow 产品摄影提示

**作者**: [Lloyd Creates](https://x.com/lloydcreates/status/2021984673216209395)  **日期**: 2026-02-12  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂的产品摄影提示，重点是生成一个浮空产品，该产品具有哑光黑色和金属银色饰面，居中放置在一个单一、连续、起伏的背景表面上，该表面具有精细的罗纹纹理和无缝的双色渐变。

![Chrome Ripple Flow 产品摄影提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964542027_zvtlha_HA-HvY7XwAAasmn.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_request": {
    "subject": "{argument name="product name" default="PRODUCT"}",
    "product_finish": {
      "primary": "matte black with subtle light absorption",
      "secondary": "polished metallic silver with mirror-like reflections",
      "treatment": "duotone — matte black body with metallic silver accents, trim, edges, or panel insets"
    },
    "composition": {
      "placement": "dead center, full view, floating suspended within the folded surface environment",
      "scale": "product occupies roughly 30-40% of the frame",
      "constraints": [
        "product must be entirely visible with no cropping",
        "no pedestals, stands, platforms, or ground planes",
        "the surface folds frame the product but never obscure more than 10% of it",
        "product is the sharpest element in the scene"
      ]
    },
    "background_environment": {
      "description": "A single continuous undulating surface that fills the entire frame, folding over and around itself in large voluminous waves — like a massive sheet of pleated metallic silk or a single machined metal panel that has been softly twisted and draped. This is NOT multiple separate ribbons or strands. It is ONE connected surface.",
      "base_color": "{argument name="deep background color" default="INSERT DEEP BACKGROUND COLOR visible in crevices — e.g. pure black, midnight navy"}",
      "surface_color_1": "{argument name="gradient color A" default="INSERT GRADIENT COLOR A — e.g. soft lavender, warm copper, pearl rose"}",
      "surface_color_2": "[INSERT GRADIENT COLOR B — e.g. deep indigo, cobalt blue, violet]",
      "color_behavior": "The two colors blend in a smooth continuous gradient across the single surface, shifting based on the surface's curvature and light angle. Where the surface faces the light it shows color_1, where it curves away it transitions to color_2. The transition is seamless with no hard edges or stripes.",
      "surface_texture": {
        "type": "fine parallel ribs embossed into the surface — like the grooves on a vinyl record or finely pleated accordion fabric",
        "rib_description": "extremely fine, uniform, tightly spaced parallel lines that follow the flow direction of the surface. The ribs are a TEXTURE on the surface, not separate objects. They create a subtle corrugated micro-relief that catches light along each tiny ridge.",
        "rib_density": "very high — approximately 50-100 visible lines per inch of surface, creating a dense linear grain",
        "rib_depth": "shallow — the ribs are subtle surface detail, not deep cuts. They create gentle highlight-shadow alternation across the surface"
      },
      "surface_form": {
        "fold_style": "large, smooth, voluminous folds like draped heavy silk — broad sweeping curves with gentle twists",
        "fold_count": "3-5 major folds visible, each one wide and generous, NOT many small tangled ribbons",
        "fold_behavior": "folds overlap softly, tucking under and over each other with smooth transitions. Where folds meet they create dee"
```

### 48. 磨砂玻璃手部的空灵产品视觉图

**作者**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X/status/2021462365146116101)  **日期**: 2026-02-11  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于在明亮的工作室环境中生成逼真的产品视觉效果。其主要特点是：抽象地表现了双手从半透明磨砂玻璃层后面伸出，营造出一种漫射模糊效果，而主要产品则保持超清晰并居中。

![磨砂玻璃手部的空灵产品视觉图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770878346292_9816kb_HA2tSKqaAAMrpAl.jpg)
![磨砂玻璃手部的空灵产品视觉图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770878346232_nv1fxm_HA2tSVAbsAATUGH.jpg)
![磨砂玻璃手部的空灵产品视觉图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770878346291_5ffac6_HA2tSEfaAAYCnhf.jpg)

```
{
 "task": "photorealistic_product_visual",
 "input": {
 "reference_image": "USER_UPLOADED_IMAGE",
 "preserve_product_identity": true,
 "preserve_label_text": true,
 "preserve_object_shape": true,
 "preserve_centered_composition": true
 },
 "scene": {
 "environment": "high-key studio",
 "background": "pure white seamless",
 "negative_space": "very high",
 "depth_of_field": "layered depth with strong subject isolation"
 },
 "subject": {
 "primary_object": "single product object",
 "position": "perfectly centered, floating",
 "orientation": "upright",
 "scale": "natural product scale",
 "clarity": "ultra-sharp, high micro-contrast"
 },
 "human_elements": {
 "hands": {
 "count": 2,
 "layering": "positioned behind a frosted glass surface",
 "visual_effect": "frosted glass diffusion, milky blur, softened edges",
 "transparency": "semi-opaque",
 "focus": "intentionally out of focus",
 "gesture": "slow, delicate, abstract reach",
 "interaction": "no contact with the product"
 }
 },

### 53. 流体 Chrome 扭曲产品渲染

**作者**: [Lloyd Creates](https://x.com/lloydcreates/status/2020875838820884854)  **日期**: 2026-02-09  **语言**: en

> 一个高度技术化、结构化的提示，用于生成产品可视化，采用“流体镀铬扭曲”效果，产品在纯黑色的虚空背景下，溶解成光滑、流动的虹彩蓝银液态金属垂直条纹，强调柔和的渐变和无硬边。

![流体 Chrome 扭曲产品渲染](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706179087_rds2wr_HAuXaHaXoAApqk-.jpg)

```
{
  "product_type": "{argument name=\"product type\" default=\"[PRODUCT]\"}",
  "prompt": "A [product_type] floating against a pure black void background (#000000). The product is small and centered in frame with generous black negative space on all sides, the product occupies no more than 50% of the frame and is never cropped. The product is visualized through a liquid vertical streak effect, as if the product has been melted and stretched into smooth, flowing vertical streaks of liquid metal. The streaks are buttery smooth, fluid, and organic like mercury or molten silver flowing downward. Each streak blends and bleeds softly into the next with no hard edges, no sharp block corners, no rigid geometry. The vertical streaks have varying thickness and luminosity, creating a sense of depth and dimensionality. The liquid streaks glow with cool monochromatic {argument name=\"color tone\" default=\"blue-silver\"} iridescent tones, think liquid mercury under blue light. The streaks flow smoothly with gentle luminous gradients, bright specular highlights fading into deep shadow. The effect is contained within the product's general silhouette shape with pure black void surrounding it. The overall impression should be a product dissolving into smooth vertical streams of liquid light. No hard edges, no blocky slats, no rigid bars.",
  "negative_prompt": "hard edges, sharp corners, blocky slats, rigid bars, chrome blocks, machined metal, solid geometric shapes, cropped product, cut off edges, radial pattern, circular rings, horizontal lines, warm colors, red, orange, yellow, green, colored background, flat lighting, matte surface",
  "style_parameters": {
    "background_color": "#000000 pure black void",
    "effect": "smooth liquid vertical streaks, fluid mercury-like, buttery soft, no hard edges",
    "effect_color": "iridescent monochromatic liquid blue-silver #C0C0C0",
    "pattern_type": "flowing liquid metal vertical streaks with soft gradients — NOT rigid blocks or bars",
    "product_framing": "centered, small in frame, max 50% canvas, NEVER cropped, generous black space",
    "product_color": "liquid mercury blue-silver iridescent",
    "lighting": "smooth luminous gradients, soft specular highlights, liquid light quality"
  }
}
```

### 55. 工业棱镜玻璃产品视觉图

**作者**: [Lloyd Creates](https://x.com/lloydcreates/status/2020332873736196341)  **日期**: 2026-02-08  **语言**: en

> 一个高度技术化的 JSON 提示，用于生成具有“棱镜工业极简主义”风格的产品视觉效果。它指定了一个由多个独立的垂直亚克力/玻璃层构成、带有气隙并由不锈钢螺栓固定在一起的产品结构。目标是实现分散的光谱高光和锐利的焦散，背景为无缝纯色，确保产品看起来像是悬浮的。

![工业棱镜玻璃产品视觉图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770619745747_mmcc8t_HAmpqr7WMAA6xib.jpg)

```
{
  "request": {
    "product": "{argument name="product name" default="[PRODUCT HERE]"}",
    "background_color": "{argument name="background color" default="#59925C"}",
    "style": "prismatic_industrial_minimalism",
    "visual_elements": {
      "structure": "multiple separate vertical acrylic layers forming the product silhouette — each layer is a distinct flat panel with visible air gaps between them, like slices of the product spaced apart",
      "material": "high-clarity glass with rainbow prismatic iridescent tint",
      "hardware": "stainless steel through-bolts with visible internal Allen hexagonal socket heads — bolts pass through all layers front to back, holding them together with visible spacing",
      "orientation": "strictly upright vertical placement, full object visibility",
      "lighting": "dispersive spectral highlights and sharp caustics"
    },
    "composition": {
      "frame": "wide shot, no cropping, centered full-product view",
      "camera_angle": "eye-level studio perspective, slightly angled to reveal gaps between layers",
      "depth_of_field": "deep enough to maintain focus on hardware details",
      "background": "seamless solid #59925C background with no floor, surface, pedestal, platform, table, shadow ground, or horizon line — the product floats against a uniform single-color field",
      "grounding": "no visible ground plane, no reflective surface beneath the product"
    },
    "rendering_details": {
      "transparency": "multi-layered refraction with thin-film interference",
      "finish": "polished edges with subtle holographic light dispersion",
      "hardware_detail": "macro-precision on hex-head bolt sockets",
      "layer_direction": "every glass/acrylic layer is strictly vertical — no horizontal slabs, curved shells, or molded forms",
      "layer_separation": "each glass panel must be visibly separated with clear air gaps — not fused or touching — bolts are the only element connecting the layers"
    }
  }
}
```

Input A is a Character with duality.

Select 4 lesser-known characters with internal conflict.

Sculpt each toy split vertically or horizontally into two contrasting halves.

Layout:

2x2 grid, toys centered, perfectly symmetrical framing, name underneath

Style Stack:
Anchor: [Split vinyl art toy]::3.5
Morphology: Bulbous toy proportions, clean bisected geometry::3

### 61. Nano Banana Pro 的图像生成提示

**作者**: [nobara](https://x.com/mityadameya/status/2018600293920063630)  **日期**: 2026-02-03  **语言**: ja

> 一个用于 Nano Banana 生成模型的提示，建议创建一个图像，描绘一位精明的投资者在不将物品从其外壳中取出的情况下处理某物，暗示着对实用性和效率的关注。该提示本身非常简短且依赖于上下文。

![Nano Banana Pro 的图像生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770187212343_a1ucbf_HAIjlOXbwAAa1Wd.jpg)

### 64. 咖啡机爆炸图产品可视化

**作者**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X/status/2018536315239997765)  **日期**: 2026-02-03  **语言**: en

> 一个高度技术性的提示，用于生成 Scarlett 滴漏式咖啡机的超逼真 3D 爆炸图可视化，要求精确的垂直对齐、详细的组件标注以及特定的材质和灯光效果，以呈现高端广告的视觉效果。

```
Create a photorealistic premium exploded-view visualization of a Scarlett drip coffee maker, fully disassembled and aligned vertically along a central axis.

All components must levitate, remain evenly spaced, perfectly centered, and aligned with precise vertical symmetry.

COMPONENT LABELING (MANDATORY)
Each component must include: 

→ A thin white or light-gray arrow / leader line
→ A clean sans-serif label placed to the right side
→ Part name + short spec (minimal, technical text)
→ Labels must NOT overlap any object
→ Arrows must point clearly to the exact component

COMPONENTS (TOP → BOTTOM, ALL FLOATING & LABELED)

1 → Upper Lid
• Matte black plastic
• Minimal geometry
→ Label: Upper Lid ➝ Heat-Resistant Plastic

2 → Water Reservoir
• Semi-transparent plastic
• Visible water scale (1–6 cups)
→ Label: Water Reservoir — 0.6 L

3 → Water Delivery System
• Thin tubes + distributor
• Clean internal engineering
→ Label: Water Flow System — Even Distribution

4 → Heating Element (TEN)
• Metal body
• Subtle warm glow
→ Label: Heating Element — 600–800 W

5 → Filter Holder
• Black plastic
• Conical drip design
→ Label: Filter Holder — Drip System

6 → Reusable Mesh Filter
• Fine stainless-steel grid
→ Label: Reusable Filter — Stainless Steel

7 → Brewing Unit
• Visible internal channels
→ Label: Brewing Chamber — Coffee Extraction

8 → Glass Carafe
• Heat-resistant transparent glass
• Black handle
→ Label: Glass Carafe — Thermal Glass

9 → Warming Plate
• Metallic heating surface
→ Label: Warming Plate — Heat Retention

10 → Base Housing & Electronics
• Rubber feet
• Power button + cable
• Internal electronics
→ Label: Base Unit — Power & Control

VISUAL EFFECTS :

• Soft steam rising from brewing unit
• Gentle warm glow from heating element
• Soft shadows beneath each floating component
• Thin guide arrows indicating assembly order

BACKGROUND : 

• Dark premium gradient (graphite → deep gray)
• Very subtle concentric circles (heat & aroma concept)
• Clean, modern kitchen-tech aesthetic

LIGHTING : 

• Soft warm key light from top-left
• Rim lighting on glass & metal edges
• No harsh or dramatic shadows

CAMERA : 

• Front-facing
• Slight top-down tilt
• Vertical 9:16
• Product occupies ~70% of the frame

STYLE & QUALITY :-

• Ultra-realistic 3D render
• Premium household appliance advertising look
• Octane / Cinema 4D style
• PBR materials (plastic, glass, metal)
• 8K, ultra-sharp, portfolio-ready

NEGATIVE PROMPT
No logos
No watermark
No clutter
No exaggerated glow
No cartoon or illustration style
```

**Related**: [[手绘素描]]、[[综合艺术]]、[[3D渲染]]

### 69. 超逼真产品变形视频提示

**作者**: [Sharon Riley](https://x.com/Just_sharon7/status/2017572013045649696)  **日期**: 2026-01-31  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于使用 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 和 Veo 3 生成一个超逼真的、固定机位的产品变形视频。场景涉及将手表无缝地、非有机地替换为静态苔藓纹理，同时严格遵守光照、颜色和摄像机移动的限制，以保持真实感。

![超逼真产品变形视频提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927649001_lm7m2t_G__bBnRbkAAkeaQ.jpg)

```
Hyper-realistic product transformation video, strict realism, no fantasy.
Locked-off camera, identical framing throughout.
Scene (0.00s – 1.20s):
A premium studio product setup. At the start, a watch is present at center frame. Within the same position, the watch is cleanly removed and replaced by a flat moss/grass texture with identical scale and footprint. The moss surface is static, flat, and texture-based only — no growth, no movement, no spreading, no organic animation.
Constraints:
– Lighting remains unchanged
– Colors remain unchanged
– Depth of field remains unchanged
– Fog, reflections, shadows, and environment remain unchanged
– No cinematic slow motion
– No glowing effects
– No seeds, vines, or plant growth
– No fantasy or surreal elements
– No camera movement
– No environmental interaction
Ultra-sharp hyper-real textures, physically accurate materials, clean studio realism, seamless object replacement, identical atmosphere before and after transformation.
```

### 76. 高端产品目录风格提示词（技术规格）

**作者**: [摆烂程序媛](https://x.com/wanerfu/status/2016693035892199858)  **日期**: 2026-01-29  **语言**: zh

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张高端产品目录图片，采用 3:4 垂直构图的详细提示。布局包括顶部的生活方式主图和底部的技术规格面板，其中包含建筑线条图和材料样本，旨在营造出精致、建筑感和宁静的设计期刊美学。

![高端产品目录风格提示词（技术规格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769755040577_518wxr_G_y7n35bYAAIK4m.jpg)

```
✓ 参考图像：使用上传的图像作为产品形式、比例、材料和整体身份的精确视觉参考。不要重新设计或重新解释产品。

✓ 布局：竖向3:4画布，背景为温暖中性纸质表面，上部为生活方式英雄区域，下部为技术规格区。

✓ 上部分：产品图像置于顶部中心，占据主导位置，周围有充足留白。

✓ 环境设置：极简主义建筑室内，自然侧光照明，柔和高对比阴影，混凝土地面，纹理灰泥墙。

✓ 渲染风格：编辑性生活摄影，高度写实，温暖柔和的高端色彩分级。

✓ 下部分：技术规格面板采用模块化网格布局。左下为建筑线条图（正视图、侧视图、四分之三俯视图），柔和红色或棕褐色细线条，最少标注。

✓ 右下：3-4个材料样本，来自产品实际材料（织物、皮革、金属、木材、塑料）。

✓ 排版：极简编辑风格，柔和黑色或深棕色，无大标题。

✓ 整体风格：设计目录/产品设计日志，建筑感、高端、平静。避免杂乱、大胆色彩、重品牌、过度装饰。

✓ 约束：不改变产品设计，不虚构材料，除非参考中有否则不添加徽标，在图纸中不使用透视失真。
```

**Related**: [[室内设计]]、[[综合建筑]]、[[综合生活]]

---

### 77. 奢华咖啡品鉴菜单布局提示

**作者**: [Willy](https://x.com/jw660227/status/2016690090387656725)  **日期**: 2026-01-29  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的提示，用于生成一个奢华、极简、同色调的咖啡品鉴菜单网页布局，详细说明了网格构成、调色板、产品展示、排版和相机细节。

![奢华咖啡品鉴菜单布局提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769755016032_wyepkb_G_y43_7bUAAIIor.jpg)

```
Luxury coffee tasting menu layout, irregular grid composition, 9:16 aspect ratio for webpage.
LAYOUT: Irregular 3x3 grid, varied cell sizes, flowing editorial arrangement
BACKGROUND: Tone-on-tone panels - alternating {argument name="color 1" default="latte beige (#F2E2D2)"}, {argument name="color 2" default="mocha brown (#D1B48F)"}, and coffee cream (#FAF5E6) creating a subtle caffeinated rhythm
PRODUCT EXPRESSION: Product only, overhead and 45-degree angles mixed, plated presentation on minimalist slate ceramics
TONE STRATEGY: Tone-on-tone - coffee colors harmonize with background tones, an ethereal blend
MAIN ELEMENTS: Individual coffee tastings - Espresso with crema foam, Cappuccino toast with gold dust, Caviar on blinis substituted with coffee caviar on biscotti, Latte with lemon twist, Mocha tartlet, each on matching plates, consistent soft lighting
TYPOGRAPHY: Bilingual - English names in elegant light serif (Didot), English/Korean below in clean sans-serif, small origin descriptions in light gray
CAMERA: Canon EOS R5, 100mm Macro for details, 50mm for full plates, soft diffused overhead lighting, side rim lighting
STYLE: Minimal + Luxury hybrid - generous whitespace, refined typography, coffee colors as primary source
Style keywords: coffee, tasting menu, tone-on-tone, luxury, webpage

A delicate handwritten signature "Willy" is elegantly placed in small letters at the bottom right corner..
```

### 78. 智能宽高比转换和构图感知

**作者**: [Ray](https://x.com/rincidium/status/2016580791321698309)  **日期**: 2026-01-28  **语言**: en

> 一个为图像处理任务设计的详细系统提示：智能地转换图像的宽高比，同时保留语义完整性和视觉连贯性。它概述了一个多步骤流程，包括分析、转换逻辑和严格的保留规则，以实现商业就绪的输出，适用于代理机构调整资产大小的工作流程。

![智能宽高比转换和构图感知](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668490760_z3cor2_G_xVgv3bgAAsl9L.jpg)

```
You are performing intelligent aspect ratio transformation with compositional awareness.

CONTEXT:
The source image exists within a specific dimensional space. Your task is to translate it into a new aspect ratio while preserving semantic integrity and visual coherence.

ANALYSIS PHASE:
- Identify the primary subject anchor point and secondary visual elements
- Map the compositional weight distribution across quadrants
- Detect edge dependencies (elements that rely on frame boundaries)
- Assess negative space utilization and breathing room requirements

TRANSFORMATION LOGIC:
- Calculate optimal subject placement using rule-of-thirds grid alignment for target ratio
- Determine extension vectors based on background continuity patterns
- Evaluate whether horizontal or vertical expansion better serves the composition
- Apply content-aware fill logic for generated regions while maintaining tonal consistency

PRESERVATION RULES:
- Typographic elements: maintain exact pixel fidelity, no scaling or repositioning unless required by new boundaries
- Brand marks and logos: preserve aspect ratio and relative positioning
- Facial features: no modification, distortion, or regeneration
- Fine details: texture patterns must flow naturally into extended regions

OUTPUT PARAMETERS:
- Seamless integration between original and generated content
- No detectable boundaries, halos, or color shifting at transition zones
- Lighting direction consistency across the full canvas
- The result must appear as if originally captured or designed at the target ratio

QUALITY THRESHOLD:
Production-ready output suitable for commercial use, print media, and high-resolution display contexts.
```

**Related**: [[综合3D]]、[[地图]]、[[名片与Logo]]

### 83. 玉石美学概念建筑静物

**作者**: [Latte](https://x.com/0xbisc/status/2016162578180002218)  **日期**: 2026-01-27  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一个微型三层中式宝塔的概念性产品风格静物画。它着重强调材料质感，具体说明了半透明的玉石般玻璃、冰蓝色调、香槟金色点缀，以及一个受程式化山水启发而设计的雕塑底座，强调了精确性和宁静感。

![玉石美学概念建筑静物](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769581922889_8og5ao_G_rZE8kXIAA6ssz.jpg)

```
A highly detailed, exquisitely crafted conceptual product-style still life of an elegant traditional Chinese pavilion, presented as a miniature architectural artwork.  The pavilion is a three-tiered pagoda structure made of semi-transparent jade-like and softly frosted glass material in refined milky white and ice-blue tones. Translucent turquoise-blue glass roofs feature delicately tapered profiles, accented with finely detailed champagne-gold ornamental edges and intricate, graceful golden flying-eave details.  A warm, subtle golden light glows gently from within the pavilion through translucent windows, creating a soft inner radiance. A small vertical blue-and-gold plaque is precisely embedded on the upper tier façade, understated yet refined.  The pavilion stands on a simplified, smooth sculptural base inspired by stylized mountains and calm water, carved from semi-transparent ice-blue crystal material. The mountain–water form is defined by elegant flowing contours, softly rounded transitions, and continuous sculptural surfaces, with restrained texture and no sharp ridges, evoking the feeling of finely polished jade, melted glass, or serene frozen waves.  The mountain–water base fully fills the bottom of the frame and is cleanly cropped by the image edge: there is no visible ground, no platform, no horizon line, and no empty bottom space. The form appears naturally immersed and continuous, extending beyond the frame rather than resting upon it.  A clean white jade staircase rises diagonally and seamlessly from within the sculptural base toward the pavilion entrance, maintaining clarity, balance, and an elegant sense of progression.  Composition is tight, refined, and immersive: the pavilion and its base occupy most of the frame, with the mountain–water structure gently pressing against the lower edge, eliminating visual emptiness while preserving calmness.  Camera: subtle low-angle, 3/4 perspective (approximately 25–30 degrees turned), with close framing to emphasize fine material quality, delicate craftsmanship, and sculptural precision.  Soft, diffused luxury studio lighting with minimal hard shadows. High realism, shallow depth of field. Clean white to light-gray gradient background confined to the upper area, with carefully restrained negative space. Calm, ethereal, refined, premium craftsmanship, serene and sacred atmosphere, Eastern fantasy meets modern minimalism.
```

Create an infographic image of {argument name="object" default="Tudor North Flag"}, combining a realistic photograph or photorealistic render of the object with technical annotation overlays placed directly on top.

Use black ink–style line drawings and text (technical pen / architectural sketch look) on a pure white studio background.

Include:
•Key component labels
•Internal cutaway or exploded-view outlines (where relevant)
•Measurements, dimensions, and scale markers
•Material callouts and quantities
•Arrows indicating function, force, or flow (air, sound, power, pressure, movement)
•Simple schematic or sectional diagrams where applicable

Place the title {argument name="object title" default="[OBJECT]"} inside a hand-drawn technical annotation box in one corner.

Style & layout rules:
•The real object remains clearly visible beneath the annotations
•Annotations look hand-sketched, technical, and architectural
•Clean composition with balanced negative space
•Educational, museum-exhibit / engineering-manual vibe

Visual style:
Minimal technical illustration aesthetic.
Black linework layered over realistic imagery.
Precise but slightly hand-drawn feel.

Color palette:
Pure white background.
Black annotation lines and text only.
No colors.

Output:
Ultra-crisp
Social-feed optimized
No watermark
```

      "Heavy noise",

    ],

The image quality is intentionally degraded, with strong motion blur, digital smearing, compression artifacts, heavy noise, scan lines, and subtle fisheye distortion warping the frame edges, making fine details indistinct and stretched. The Subject is centered from mid-torso upward, looking up toward the camera with the head tilted back; facial features are largely obscured by blur and artifacts, though dark oversized sunglasses dominate the face, reflecting ambient light, and the mouth appears open with the tongue faintly visible. One hand is raised toward the camera with the middle finger extended, clearly readable in silhouette but softened and ghosted by motion and low clarity, conveying a relaxed yet defiant posture. Harsh, flat fluorescent lighting pro

### 89. 超现实的迷你品客薯片罐滑雪场景视频提示

**作者**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0/status/2015684966567592275)  **日期**: 2026-01-26  **语言**: en

> 这是一个详细的视频生成提示，用于描述一个超现实、充满趣味的场景：在一个微型冬季景观中，薯片从品客（Pringles）薯片罐中溢出，形成了一条供微型滑雪者使用的滑雪道。该提示详细说明了运动、摄像机工作（电影级微距镜头）、灯光以及产品稳定性的限制。

![超现实的迷你品客薯片罐滑雪场景视频提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495307022_wtccwg_G_kmwtbaQAApiCX.jpg)

```
Prompt: A surreal miniature winter scene in the mountains. A large blue Pringles can lies tipped over in the snow, spilling potato chips that form a winding snowboard track. Tiny snowboarders ride smoothly along the curved chip-and-snow path, carving through the slope. Snow-covered mountains and clear blue sky in the background. Bright daylight, playful fantasy tone, ultra-realistic textures, crisp snow detail, shallow depth of field.
Motion (Primary):
Mini snowboarders glide downhill in smooth arcs, carving gently along the curved track.
Secondary Motion:
Loose chip pieces tumble slowly in the snow, fine snow particles kick up behind the boards, light powder spray follows turns.
Camera:
Cinematic macro shot, slow tracking follow along the snowboard path, low angle close to the snow surface, gentle parallax as the camera moves forward, stable and smooth.
Style & Lighting:
Bright natural winter daylight, clean contrast, vibrant product colors, soft highlights on snow, realistic shadows, whimsical commercial aesthetic.
Constraints:
Keep Pringles can and logo shape stable and readable.
Snowboarders remain miniature and proportional.
No distortion of chips, no melting snow, no object duplication.
Negative Prompt:
warped logo, unreadable text, stretched can, broken snowboarders, extra limbs, chaotic motion, shaky camera, flicker, excessive motion blur, glitch artifacts.
```

### 90. 低保真闭路电视监控画面图像

**作者**: [Melisa♡](https://x.com/xmliisu/status/2015679962573889621)  **日期**: 2026-01-26  **语言**: en

> 一个独特的提示，旨在生成故意降级、低保真度的图像，类似于闭路电视监控画面。它侧重于运动模糊、噪点和低分辨率等伪影，描绘了一个在杂乱零售店中姿态 defiant 的主体。

![低保真闭路电视监控画面图像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495326188_slg07g_G_kiPLRWEAE2CHc.jpg)

```
{
  "image_description": {
    "title": "Surveillance Feed: Defiant Subject in Retail Shop",
    "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
    "mood": "Raw, gritty, confrontational, authentic"
  },
  "visual_elements": {
    "subject": {
      "framing": "Centered from mid-torso upward",
      "pose": "Head tilted back looking up at camera, relaxed yet defiant posture",
      "action": "Hand raised with middle finger extended (silhouette, ghosted by motion)",
      "facial_features": "Largely obscured by blur, mouth open with tongue faintly visible",
      "apparel": "Dark oversized sunglasses reflecting ambient light"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Cramped retail shop interior",
      "foreground": "Cluttered checkout counter, papers, white shopping bag with red rope handles",
      "background": "Densely packed shelves with small items, souvenirs, and figurines (abstracted by low resolution)"
    }
  },
  "technical_specifications": {
    "camera_perspective": "High-mounted, steep downward angle, top-down CCTV view",
    "lens_distortion": "Subtle fisheye warping at frame edges",
    "lighting": "Harsh flat fluorescent, blown highlights, dull shadows",
    "color_grading": "Cool green-blue cast, uneven color reproduction, visible banding, reduced dynamic range"
  },
  "image_fidelity": {
    "quality": "Intentionally degraded, low-fidelity",
    "artifacts": [
      "Strong motion blur",
      "Digital smearing",
      "Compression artifacts",
      "Heavy noise",
      "Scan lines"
    ],
    "sharpness": "Low perceived sharpness, distinct details stretched and indistinct"
  },
  "full_prompt_text": "A heavily distorted, low-fidelity surveillance-style image depicts the Subject standing behind a cramped retail checkout counter inside a cluttered shop, captured from a high-mounted camera angled steeply downward in a top-down CCTV perspective. The image quality is intentionally degraded, with strong motion blur, digital smearing, compression artifacts, heavy noise, scan lines, and subtle fisheye distortion warping the frame edges, making fine details indistinct and stretched. The Subject is centered from mid-torso upward, looking up toward the camera with the head tilted back; facial features are largely obscured by blur and artifacts, though dark oversized sunglasses dominate the face, reflecting ambient light, and the mouth appears open with the tongue faintly visible. One hand is raised toward the camera with the middle finger extended, clearly readable in silhouette but softened and ghosted by motion and low clarity, conveying a relaxed yet defiant posture. The foreground checkout counter is cluttered with papers and a white shopping bag with red rope handles, while the background shelves are densely packed with small items, souvenirs, and figurines that blend into abstract shapes due to low resolution and noise. Harsh, flat fluorescent lighting pro"
```

**Related**: [[手绘素描]]、[[综合艺术]]、[[微缩模型与立体模型]]

### 96. 电影级混合现实第一人称视角超市提示词

**作者**: [Sharon Riley](https://x.com/Just_sharon7/status/2014499743301538082)  **日期**: 2026-01-23  **语言**: en

> 一个 JSON 提示，用于生成一个电影般的混合现实场景，该场景以第一人称视角（POV）展现现代超市货架。重点是一个手握着一瓶鲜奶，并增强了全息 UI 元素，例如显示脂肪含量和价格趋势的浮动数据卡，以及在余光中出现的细微购物清单。

```
{
  "scene_type": "immersive_pov",
  "environment": {
    "location": "modern supermarket aisle",
    "lighting": "bright store lighting",
    "visual_style": "hyper-realistic mixed reality",
    "depth_of_field": "natural"
  },
  "camera": {
    "perspective": "first-person POV",
    "focus": "hand holding milk bottle"
  },
  "main_object": {
    "item": "fresh milk bottle",
    "position": "center foreground",
    "interaction": "held in hand"
  },
  "augmented_reality_ui": {
    "holographic_card": {
      "position": "floating near bottle",
      "design": "clean, minimalist",
      "data": {
        "fat_content": "{argument name="fat content" default="3.5%"}",
        "expiry_countdown": "visible",
        "price_trend": "30 days"
      }
    },
    "shopping_list": {
      "position": "left peripheral vision",
      "orientation": "vertical",
      "status": "partially checked",
      "opacity": "subtle"
    },
    "product_price_tags": {
      "applies_to": "other dairy products",
      "style": "subtle floating AR labels"
    }
  },
  "aesthetic": {
    "ui_style": "minimalist AR interface",
    "realism_level": "high",
    "immersion": "cinematic mixed reality"
  }
}
```

### 97. Lovart 品牌的多步设计生成提示

**作者**: [KAWAI](https://x.com/kawai_design/status/2014272630833226237)  **日期**: 2026-01-22  **语言**: ja

> 一个全面、多步骤的工作流程，使用设计代理“Lovart”（可能与 Nano Banana Pro 集成）来生成完整的品牌形象，从标志开始，延伸到设计指南、UI、网站、展位和商品。这展示了一种结构化的设计生成方法。

![Lovart 品牌的多步设计生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769149373823_avjhxj_G_QiCWtawAAkGgW.jpg)

```
鮮やかな{argument name="色1" default="エメラルドグリーン"}と鮮やかな{argument name="色2" default="ブルー"}のグラデーションがベースカラーの「{argument name="企業名" default="Lovart"}」という企業のロゴマーク

このロゴマークからカラーパレットとフォントのデザインガイドラインを生成

このサービスのアプリケーションUIデザインを生成して。PC版とスマートフォン版

このサービスを紹介するWebサイトのデザイン。PC版とスマートフォン版

このサービスの展示会用ブースのデザインイメージ

このサービスのグッズデザイン。Tシャツ、パーカー、キャップ、ノート、ステッカー
```

### 98. 品牌视觉的详细故事板提示

**作者**: [Lovart 公式 (ラブアート)](https://x.com/lovart_jp/status/2014261792491647076)  **日期**: 2026-01-22  **语言**: ja

> 一个高度详细、多帧的提示，专为 Nano Banana Pro 设计，用于生成一个干净、专业的 3x3 故事板网格，以用于品牌组合。它强调所有九个帧中产品标识、颜色和比例的一致性，侧重于构图、材质和视觉节奏，而非叙事。

![品牌视觉的详细故事板提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769149374673_qpygep_G_QW86Za4AANkA3.jpg)

```
3×3 [比率] のクリーンなストーリーボードグリッドに、9 つの [比率] サイズのパネルを [4:5] の比率で配置します。

参考画像を製品のベースイメージとして使用します。製品、パッケージデザイン、ブランディング、素材、色、比率、全体的なアイデンティティは、参考画像と完全に同じにしてください。製品はすべてのフレームで明確に認識できる必要があります。ラベル、ロゴ、比率は完全に同じである必要があります。

このストーリーボードは、ブランディングポートフォリオ用の高級デザイナーによるモックアッププレゼンテーションです。リアリズムやライフスタイルのナラティブではなく、形状、構成、素材、視覚的なリズムに焦点を当てています。全体的な外観は、キュレーションされた、編集された、デザイン主導の印象を与える必要があります。

フレーム 1:
クリーンなスタジオセットアップで、製品を正面から撮影したヒーローショット。ニュートラルな背景、バランスの取れた構図、落ち着いた自信に満ちた製品のプレゼンテーション。

フレーム2：
製品の中心にフォーカスを合わせたクローズアップショット。表面の質感、素材、印刷のディテールに焦点を当てています。

フレーム3：
ブランドと製品カテゴリーに自然に溶け込む環境に配置された参考製品。製品のデザイン要素と色彩からインスピレーションを得たスタジオセッティングです。

フレーム4：
ニュートラルなスタジオの背景に、製品の使用またはインタラクションの様子が写っています。手やインタラクション要素は最小限に抑えられ、パッケージのスタイルにマッチした外観です。

フレーム5：
複数の製品を上面から等角投影し、正確な幾何学的順序で配置したアイソメトリック構図です。すべての製品が同じ上面から等角投影され、均等な間隔で配置され、すっきりと整理され、グラフィックな印象を与えます。

フレーム6：
参考画像のカラーパレットにマッチしたニュートラルな背景に、製品がわずかに傾けて浮かんでいます。意図的に角度をつけて浮かんでいるため、製品は空間に自然に浮かんでいます。

フレーム7：
ラベル、エッジ、テクスチャ、または素材の挙動といった特定のディテールに焦点を当てた、極めてクローズアップのショットです。

フレーム8：
製品は、予想外でありながらも美的に力強いセッティングの中にあり、大胆でエディトリアルな印象を与え、視覚的に印象的です。

予想外でありながら、高度に様式化されたセッティング。スタジオを拠点とし、デザイナー主導で制作。ブランドイメージを高める大胆な構図。

フレーム9：
洗練されたデザイナーのセッティングの中に置かれた製品の使用シーンを映し出すワイドな構図。無駄のない小道具、コントロールされたスタイリング、そしてシリーズの他の作品との統一感。

カメラとスタイル：
リアルなカメラルックを備えた、超高画質のスタジオ撮影。フレームごとに異なるカメラアングルとフレーミング。被写界深度、正確な照明、正確な素材と反射。照明のロジック、カラーパレット、ムード、そしてビジュアルランゲージは、9つのパネル全体で一貫性を保ち、1つのシリーズとして統一する必要があります。

出力:
境界線、テキスト、キャプション、透かしのない、すっきりとした 3×3 グリッド。
```

**Related**: [[综合生活]]

---

**作者**: [Sibo Esenkova](https://x.com/SiboEsenkova/status/2014018557487530068)  **日期**: 2026-01-21  **语言**: en

### 100. 教育商品宇宙立体模型提示

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2013939130263339032)  **日期**: 2026-01-21  **语言**: en

> 一个教育性的、高度结构化的提示模板，旨在生成一个“商品宇宙”立体模型等距桌面摄影图像。它指示 AI 将选定的商品（如咖啡或黄金）解构为其核心、种类和历史运输方式，并将它们布置在一个抛光的木板上，以详细的博物馆风格展示。

![教育商品宇宙立体模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063198703_3k4ai0_G_ERfQVXgAAaud_.jpg)
![教育商品宇宙立体模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063198723_xmw01v_G_ERhPUW4AAo_mG.jpg)

```
<instruction> for {argument name="commodity" default="Coffee"}

Input A is a Historic Commodity or Resource (e.g., Spices, Tea, Silk, Coffee, Gold).
Deconstruct the commodity into 3 Educational Assets:
     The Core :  Identify the most common or valuable raw form.
         (e.g., Spices -> A pile of Black Peppercorns. Tea -> A mound of Black Tea leaves. Gold -> A large Nugget). 
     The Varieties:  Identify 4-5 distinct variations or colors.
         (e.g., Spices -> Red Paprika, Yellow Turmeric, Brown Cinnamon. Tea -> Green, White, Oolong, Matcha). 
     The Transit :  Identify the historical method of transport.
         (e.g., Camel Caravans, East Indiaman Ships, Steam Trains). 

  2. Container
Goal: "Commodity Universe" Educational Diorama.
     The Base:  A large, square   Polished Walnut or Oak Board   sitting on a library table.
     The Layout:  A radial/circular design in the center, flanked by narrative vignettes in the corners.

  3. The Centerpiece
     The Metaphor:  The commodity is the center of the world.
     The Sun:  A massive, textured pile of the "Core" material (Step 1) sits in the exact center.
     The Orbit:  Inlaid gold or brass rings ripple out from the center.
     The Planets:  Smaller mounds or spheres of the "Varieties" (Step 1) orbit the center, creating a colorful spectrum of textures (powders, grains, solids).

  4. Narrative Corners 
     The Origin (Top Corners):  Miniature dioramas sculpted directly onto the board showing the harvesting process (e.g., tiny figures picking tea leaves, mining gold, or shaking spice trees).
     The Journey (Bottom Corners):  Miniature dioramas showing the "Transit" (Step 1).
         Detail:  Use   Resin   for water (ships) or   Sand   for deserts (camels).

  5. The Footer:  
     Placement:  Along the bottom edge of the board.
     Format:  Three or four rectangular   Wooden Plaques   embedded in the table.
     Content:  The name of a specific variety (e.g., "Cinnamon") engraved in serif text, with a physical sample of that ingredient piled on the plaque.

  Output:   ONE image, 1:1 Aspect Ratio, Isometric Tabletop Photography, "Museum Display" aesthetic, Warm Tones.
</instruction>
```

**Related**: [[微缩模型与立体模型]]、[[综合3D]]、[[综合设计]]

---

### 103. 抽象中国山水微缩模型提示

**作者**: [MarioTan](https://x.com/TanShilong/status/2013607884643606679)  **日期**: 2026-01-20  **语言**: zh

> 一个详细的图像生成提示，旨在将任何物体渲染成仿佛完全由粗羊毛手工编织而成。该提示强调纹理、可见的针脚、麻花针织图案以及舒适实用的美学，适用于创作异想天开又逼真的纺织艺术图像。用户需要在括号中输入所需的物体。

![针织纱线物体生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890733416_f2tclp_G_DlR6gWYAE3UZP.jpg)
![针织纱线物体生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890733497_p4jibb_G_Dlh19WcAAqKYa.jpg)

![针织纱线物体生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890734669_j9rf60_G_DlR6NWYAAFnge.jpg)

```
두툼한 양모 원사로 완전히 손으로 짠 것처럼 렌더링 된 [{argument name="물건" default="전자렌지"}] 부드러운 공예임에도 불구하고 믿을 수 없을 정도로 기능적으로 보입니다. 눈에 보이는 스 티치, 그립 영역의 케이블 니트 패턴, 유연성이 필요 한 리브, 원사 끝은 깔끔하게 집어넣습니다.

아늑한 라이프스타일 배경이나 깨끗한 양모 질감의 스튜디오에서 촬영. 원사 질감, 수제 품질, 기계의 터 무니없는 아늑함을 강조하는 따뜻하고 부드러운 조 명. 스티치 디테일, 따뜻한 포화 섬유 색상, 라이프스 타일 제품 미학, 초고해상도, 하드메이드 소프트에 대 한 날카로운 초점
```

### 110. Cozy Knit 工业设计提示

**作者**: [Alexandra Aisling](https://x.com/AllaAisling/status/2012909092210381048)  **日期**: 2026-01-18  **语言**: en

> 此提示旨在将任何指定对象渲染成仿佛完全由粗羊毛线手工编织而成，融合了斯堪的纳维亚的 hygge 美学与工业设计。它强调可见的针脚、绞花编织图案、温暖的灯光和超高分辨率，以突出纱线的柔软质感。

![Cozy Knit 工业设计提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804226001_g1x8cv_G-7OpVTWwAAYDCQ.jpg)

```
An {argument name="object" default="[OBJECT]"} rendered as if entirely hand-knitted from chunky wool yarn, impossibly functional-looking despite being soft craft. Visible stitches, cable knit patterns on grip areas, ribbing where flexibility is needed, yarn ends neatly tucked. Positioned against a cozy lifestyle backdrop or clean wool-texture studio. Scandinavian hygge meets industrial design. Warm soft lighting emphasizing the yarn texture, the handmade quality, the absurd coziness of machinery. Sharp focus on stitch detail, warm saturated fiber colors, lifestyle product aesthetic, ultra-high resolution, the hard made soft.

### 113. 奢华韩服产品模型（对称平铺）

**作者**: [Willy](https://x.com/jw660227/status/2012485594723848458)  **日期**: 2026-01-17  **语言**: en

> 一个高度具体的提示，旨在生成一个对称、居中平铺构图的传统韩服奢侈品模型。它要求无缝的纯白色背景，并详细说明了从中央的深红色丝绸短上衣（Jeogori）到周围配饰（如福袋（Bokjumeoni）和发簪（Binyeo））的每件物品的摆放、颜色和纹理，旨在呈现一种平衡、具有编辑风格的商业摄影效果。

![奢华韩服产品模型（对称平铺）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717573973_la4jzd_G-3I-OnXgAAXBks.jpg)

```
A luxury Korean traditional Hanbok (한복) product mockup with perfectly balanced centered composition on seamless white background.

CANVAS & BACKGROUND - CRITICAL:
- Seamless infinity white backdrop fills entire frame edge to edge
- Background extends from corner to corner with no visible borders
- Clean warm white (#FFFAF5) continuous uniform tone across full canvas
- No vignetting, no falloff, no darkening at edges
- All four corners identical in color and brightness
- Even exposure across entire image from left to right, top to bottom
COMPOSITION - SYMMETRICAL CENTERED LAYOUT:
- Perfect center axis alignment
- Equal visual weight on left and right sides
- Products arranged in triangular hierarchy
- Minimum 10% margin between products and frame edges
BACK ROW (Top Center):
- CENTER-BACK: Matte black gift box with gold Dancheong border, 연꽃문 lotus embossed, "한스타일 Hstyle" in gold
- LEFT-BACK: Cream shopping bag with gold Taegeuk symbol
- RIGHT-BACK: Open box showing cream silk lining with gold crane pattern
MIDDLE ROW (Center Hero):
- EXACT CENTER: Crimson red silk Hanbok Jeogori (저고리) with gold peony embroidery on cream silk cloth, sleeves spread symmetrically, white collar (동정) visible
FRONT ROW (Evenly Spaced):
- LEFT: Traditional fan (부채) with plum blossom
- CENTER-LEFT: Plum blossom sprig
- CENTER: Royal blue Bokjumeoni (복주머니) with gold 福
- CENTER-RIGHT: Gold Binyeo (비녀) on cream cushion
- RIGHT: Plum blossom sprig
LIGHTING:
- Soft diffused overhead lighting
- Even illumination including all corners and edges
- No directional shadows toward frame edges
- Consistent brightness across full frame
CAMERA:
- Shot straight-on, camera perfectly centered
- 4:5 aspect ratio
- Products composed with safe margin from all edges
- Full frame background coverage
STYLE: Balanced editorial luxury, Korean heritage, commercial product photography
Negative prompt: vignetting, dark corners, uneven background, cropped edges, gradient falloff, visible backdrop edges, inconsistent lighting at borders
A stylish handwritten signature "Willy" in small gold letters at bottom right corner.
```

### 116. 爆炸图豪华手表信息图提示

**作者**: [SANI BULA](https://x.com/SaniBulaAI/status/2011795602582225329)  **日期**: 2026-01-15  **语言**: en

> 生成奢侈腕表动态序列和两张相关图片的双部分提示。动态提示描述了腕表组件垂直分离。图片 1 是一张高端产品照片，图片 2 是一张超逼真的垂直信息图，展示了白色背景下解构的内部组件（表镜、指针、机芯、表壳）。

```
Motion Prompt:
The watch components gently separate in a vertical exploded motion, maintaining perfect symmetry and alignment. Motion is smooth, precise, and mechanical.

Image 1 :-
A premium product photograph of a stainless steel luxury watch. Clean dial, polished metal bracelet. Shot on a pure white background with soft reflections and shadows. High-end horology aesthetic, ultra-sharp focus, 8K resolution.

Image 2 :-
Create a hyper-realistic exploded vertical infographic composition of a luxury watch. From top to bottom: sapphire crystal glass, watch hands and dial, mechanical movement gears, casing, bracelet links. White background, soft studio lighting, clean technical labels, premium watchmaking aesthetic, 8K quality.
```

> 一个用于生成现代人体工学椅的彩色、极简主义爆炸图的提示。它指定了风格（工业设计，扁平但具有 3D 效果）、构图（垂直分离的组件），并要求使用简洁的无衬线字体清晰标注所有部件（头枕、脚轮等）。这对于教育内容或产品营销图表非常有用。

### 124. 销售内容缩略图生成提示（大脑/技巧/笔记）

**作者**: [まみや@AIで1.7億](https://x.com/akihitomamiya/status/2010592584083849622)  **日期**: 2026-01-12  **语言**: ja

> 一个结构化的系统提示，旨在与 Nano Banana Pro 配合使用，为 Brain、Tips 和 Note 等在线内容平台生成高质量、具有“销售力”且引人注目的缩略图。该提示将角色定义为专业的平面设计师，并提供了详细的设计风格指南，包括布局、配色方案、排版以及自定义所需的输入字段。

![销售内容缩略图生成提示（大脑/技巧/笔记）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768319238633_so1f3r_G-SQYQjaoAATtF_.jpg)

```
# Role

あなたは、Brain、Tips、noteで「売れる」アイキャッチ画像を作成するプロのグラフィックデザイナーです。

# Task

以下の【タイトル】と【サブキャッチコピー】を使い、視認性が高く、権威性と期待感を感じさせる高画質なサムネイルを作成してください。

# Design Style

- 構成：添付画像のレイアウトをベースにする。

1. [最上部]：左上に、角丸の黒い帯（バッジ）を配置し、そこに【実績・緊急性ワード】を記載。

2. [中央上部]：【サブキャッチコピー】を、太字の白文字（オレンジや黄色の縁取り）で配置。

3. [中央]：メインの【タイトル】を、画面を横断するように巨大な太文字で配置。文字は「黄色から白へのグラデーション」や「ネオン発光」など、背景色に映える最も目立つ色にし、多重の縁取りとドロップシャドウで立体感を出す。

4. [下部]：左右に2つの「特典ボックス（長方形）」を配置。それぞれの上に「特典01」「特典02」と書かれたリボンやバッジを乗せる。ボックス内には【特典内容】を記載。

5. [装飾]：画面の左右どちらかの端に、テーマに合わせた可愛らしい、または知的なキャラクター（人物や動物）を配置。

- 色彩：【希望のメインカラー】を基調とした、高彩度でエネルギッシュな配色。
- 背景：単色ではなく、テーマに関連するアイコン（例：SNS、お金、グラフなど）が散りばめられた、奥行きのあるグラフィカルな背景。

# Input Data

- 【メインカラー】：{argument name="メインカラー" default="青系"}
- 【実績・緊急性ワード】：{argument name="実績・緊急性ワード" default="参入5日で10万達成！"}
- 【サブキャッチコピー】：{argument name="サブキャッチコピー" default="商品作りなし！実績なしでOK！最短1ヶ月で"}
- 【タイトル】：{argument name="タイトル" default="Threads × アフィ 攻略講座"}
- 【特典01内容】：{argument name="特典01内容" default="実際に売れた投稿10日分"}
- 【特典02内容】：{argument name="特典02内容" default="AI自動生成ツール付き"}

# Constraints

- 日本語のテキストは正確に描写すること。
- フォントは太く、力強いゴシック体やデザインフォントを使用すること。
- 16:9の比率で出力すること。
__________________________
```

**Related**: [[综合3D]]、[[综合设计]]、[[Q版角色]]

> 为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 生成豪华韩式品鉴菜单的编辑布局的详细提示。该提示指定了 2x2 网格构图、与菜肴相协调的单色配色方案（深红色、赭色、青瓷色），以及四道主要韩式菜肴的详细描述，旨在呈现由 Annie Leibovitz 拍摄的“极简 + 奢华混合”风格。

![奢华韩式品鉴菜单编辑布局提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767967512845_4qlotn_G-IlkiUb0AAaalj.jpg)

```
Luxury Korean tasting menu, editorial layout, 2+2 large grid composition, 4:5 aspect ratio.

LAYOUT: 2x2 large grid, with two hero images on top and two supporting images below, balanced asymmetric arrangement

BACKGROUND: Tone-on-tone panels - alternating deep crimson (#800000), ochre (#CC7722), and celadon (#ACE1AF), creating warm yet appetizing rhythm

PRODUCT EXPRESSION: Product only, overhead and 45-degree angles mixed, plated presentation on artisanal black ceramics and traditional Korean wooden trays

TONE STRATEGY: Monochrome red/brown/green - Korean dish colors harmonize with background tones, seamless blend with pops of natural food color

MAIN ELEMENTS:
Hero Image 1 (top left): {argument name="hero dish 1" default="Bossam (boiled pork belly) plated with kimchi and ssamjang (fermented soybean paste)"}
Hero Image 2 (top right): {argument name="hero dish 2" default="Bibimbap (mixed rice with vegetables and beef) with gochujang (chili pepper paste), egg yolk, and sesame oil"}
Supporting Image 1 (bottom left): Galbijjim (braised short ribs) in a dark glossy sauce with chestnuts and ginko nuts
Supporting Image 2 (bottom right): Bingsu (shaved ice dessert) with red bean paste, condensed milk, and various fruits

TYPOGRAPHY: Bilingual - English names in elegant light serif (Didot), Hangul below in clean sans-serif, small ingredient descriptions in light gray

CAMERA: Canon EOS R5, 100mm Macro for details, 50mm for full plates, soft diffused overhead lighting, butterfly lighting

STYLE: Minimal + Luxury hybrid - generous whitespace, refined typography, Korean dish colors as only color source, shot by Annie Leibovitz

### 130. 自主金融艺术家 3D 股票可视化提示

**作者**: [两斤](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt/status/2009147940074569970)  **日期**: 2026-01-08  **语言**: zh

> 一个复杂的多步骤 LLM 提示，专为假设的“自主金融艺术家”工具（Banana Prompt）设计。该提示指示 AI 首先检索用户指定股票代码的实时股票数据（价格、涨跌幅、原因），然后编译一个详细的图像生成提示，用于创建一个 3D 等距微缩立体模型，以可视化该股票的表现和核心产品，并使用颜色和氛围来反映收益或损失。

![自主金融艺术家 3D 股票可视化提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767967487881_6iscq0_G-HsrMyb0AEHOYn.jpg)

```
# Role: Autonomous Financial Artist
你是一个拥有实时联网能力的 3D 视觉艺术家。你的任务是根据用户提供的股票代码，获取实时数据，并生成一张“3D 轴测微缩模型”风格的数据可视化海报。

# ⚠️ CORE INSTRUCTION: SEARCH & REPLACE
你必须严格遵守“先搜索，后替换，再生成”的流程。生成的 Prompt 中**绝对不能**包含任何 `{{...}}` 格式的占位符，必须替换为具体的文本或数值。

---

## STEP 1: DATA RETRIEVAL (联网搜索)
搜索以下变量的实时数据：
1.  **[VAR_DATE]:** 今天的日期 (格式: MMM DD, e.g., JAN 07)。
2.  **[VAR_PRICE]:** 该股票当前价格。
3.  **[VAR_CHANGE]:** 今日涨跌幅 (格式: +X.X% 或 -X.X%)。
4.  **[VAR_REASON]:** 用极简短语解释今日涨跌原因 (英文, max 5 words)。
5.  **[VAR_PRODUCT]:** 该公司的核心拳头产品或标志性建筑外观。
6.  **[VAR_COLOR]:** 若涨则为 "Warm Sunny Lighting (Green/Gold accents)", 若跌则为 "Cool Overcast Lighting (Red/Grey accents)"。
7.  **[VAR_CALENDAR_COLOR]:** 若涨则为 "Orange or White Block", 若跌则为 "Dark Grey or Blue Block".

---

## STEP 2: PROMPT COMPILATION (替换占位符)
基于搜索结果，构建最终的绘图指令。请按以下逻辑填充：

**"一张精致的 3D 轴测微缩模型 (Isometric Diorama)，纯色背景。**

**1. 视觉中心 (Visual Anchor):**
场景的主体是一个微缩版的 **[VAR_PRODUCT]**，建筑顶部有该公司的 3D Logo。

**2. 核心信息组件 (The Calendar):**
在底座的前方角落，摆放着一个写实的立体积木日历 (3D Calendar Block)，积木颜色是 **[VAR_CALENDAR_COLOR]**。积木上清晰地刻着日期文字 **'[VAR_DATE]'**。
*(重要：确保日期文字清晰、笔画锐利，作为时间戳)*

**3. 环境氛围 (Data Atmosphere):**
整体光影风格是 **[VAR_COLOR]**。
* *(如果涨)*: 场景充满生机，有漂浮的上升粒子，植被翠绿。
* *(如果跌)*: 场景略显冷清，植被偏黄或有落叶，地面有少许积水。

**4. 悬浮信息层 (UI Overlay):**
在模型上方合成 AR 风格的极简标签：
* 主标签: '{{User_Stock}} **[VAR_PRICE]**'
* 副标签: '**[VAR_CHANGE]**' (带箭头)
* 底部注释: 'Note: **[VAR_REASON]**'
**"**

---

## STEP 3: EXECUTE GENERATION (执行生图)
使用 STEP 2 中已经**替换完毕**的具体描述，立刻生成图片。

---

# USER INPUT
Target Stock Code: {argument name="stock code" default="NVDA"}
```

**Related**: [[综合艺术]]、[[微缩模型与立体模型]]、[[综合3D]]

### 134. 逼真的室内透明微缩透视模型提示

**作者**: [小洲洲的AI日常](https://x.com/LZhou15365/status/2008493602310394359)  **日期**: 2026-01-06  **语言**: zh

> 这是两步提示序列的第二部分，它将之前生成的逼真室内图像作为参考。目标是将该逼真房间转换为一个高度精细、透明的微缩建筑模型或立体模型，类似于博物馆展品。该提示强调在保留精确布局和比例的同时，专注于高端工业设计美学、透明亚克力/玻璃外壳、逼真的微缩材料以及精致的内部/外部照明对比。

![逼真的室内透明微缩透视模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804127851_7f2xnk_G9-YpF7boAEz7nC.jpg)
![逼真的室内透明微缩透视模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804128173_wwjjfd_G9-YpF-a4AAoYbt.jpg)
![逼真的室内透明微缩透视模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804128251_4zd9hp_G9-YpF5aQAEHyRQ.jpg)
![逼真的室内透明微缩透视模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804132045_jxbcv8_G9-YpF5aMAAVeJC.jpg)

```
基于上传的“现实室内空间”参考图，生成一座“透明迷你小屋展示模型”。

【核心展示概念】
- 将原本的真实室内空间转化为一座“微缩比例的透明建筑模型”
- 像博物馆中展示的建筑剖面模型
- 房屋被完整封装在透明亚克力 / 玻璃外壳中
- 室内结构与家具完全可见

【结构与布局（必须严格保留）】
- 严格继承参考图中的室内布局与比例
- 墙体位置、家具摆放、动线关系完全一致
- 房间被整体缩小为迷你比例（如 1:10 / 1:12）
- 这是比例缩放，不是重新设计

【透明外壳设计】
- 外部为高透明度亚克力或玻璃材质
- 边角圆润，厚度清晰可见
- 局部采用剖切 / 切角结构，方便观察内部
- 透明外壳不遮挡主要室内视线

【室内表现（微缩但真实）】
- 所有家具按比例缩小
- 材质依然真实：木纹、布艺、金属
- 保留现实生活感，而非玩具感
- 灯具、植物、摆件清晰可见

【灯光系统（重点）】
- 室内暖色微光灯（如模型灯）
- 外部中性或冷色展示灯
- 形成内暖外冷的高级展示对比
- 轻微发光但不刺眼

【展示环境】
- 放置在极简展台 / 博物馆展示台上
- 背景干净（浅灰 / 深灰 / 黑色）
- 有真实比例参照（如展台阴影）

【视觉风格】
- 超写实
- 高级工业设计感
- 像 Apple / Muji / 建筑事务所的展示作品
- 非玩具风，非卡通风

【摄影与构图】
- 专业产品摄影或建筑模型摄影
- 中近景构图，略微俯视
- 景深，背景虚化
- 清晰对焦在透明小屋本体

【技术要求】
- 超高清细节
- 高折射率真实玻璃表现
- 正确反射与透视
- 无人物、无文字、无水印

作为艺术装置展示，具有当代设计与收藏价值
治愈、精致、让人一眼停住的视觉效果
避免玩具质感，避免塑料感，强调建筑模型与工业设计质感
高透明度、清晰折射边缘、干净玻璃
室内灯光清晰可见，像微缩模型灯光系统
```

**Related**: [[微缩模型与立体模型]]、[[室内设计]]、[[建筑摄影]]
